title: Centos7.9 Docker安装 php_fpm 7.4
meta: Centos7.9 Docker安装 php_fpm 7.4
---
* content
{:toc}

## 前言

接上文 [Centos7.9 Docker安装及相关服务实现](https://ibaiyang.github.io/blog/linux/2022/02/17/Centos7.9-Docker安装及相关服务实现.html) ，
因为有些composer的sdk包对php版本有要求，如要求 php 至少要是 7.4版，现在php已经到8.0版了，在这里说一下 Docker安装 7.4版php。

## 正文

第一次安装，想着简单一些，共用上面 php:7.1.30-fpm 的配置文件 `/etc/php` ，结果有些拓展要提前再次安装好，过程不太顺利。
理论上，应该用一个全新的环境来安装，这样彼此隔离，不会相互影响。

docker 搜索 php 资源
> docker search php

```

### 重用配置文件

创建容器并运行
```
docker run --name php-fpm-7.4 -p 9000:9000 -v /etc/php:/usr/local/etc/php -v /media/sf_www:/var/www/html -v /etc/localtime:/etc/localtime:ro --privileged=true -d php:7.4-fpm
```

```
[root@localhost ~]# docker run --name php-fpm-7.4 -p 9000:9000 -v /etc/php:/usr/local/etc/php -v /media/sf_www:/v  ar/www/html -v /etc/localtime:/etc/localtime:ro --privileged=true -d php:7.4-fpm

[root@localhost ~]#
[root@localhost ~]#

进入容器
>  docker exec -it php-fpm-7.4 /bin/bash

查看版本：
> php -v

查看拓展：
> php -m

```

可以看到，Unable to load dynamic library，动态库丢失，下面要提前安装好。

#### 权限

查看共享文件夹所属组，新建用户组，把服务用户追增到该用户组下。
> groupadd -g 995 vboxsf
> 
> usermod -aG vboxsf www-data

```

#### mysqli拓展安装

初始化php源码目录：
> docker-php-source extract 

运行上面命令后，会在`/usr/src`目录下生成一个php源码目录。

```
root@bdaa1d27444a:/var/www/html# ls -l /usr/src | grep php
-rw-r--r-- 1 root root 10418352 Mar  2 04:55 php.tar.xz
-rw-r--r-- 1 root root      833 Mar  2 04:55 php.tar.xz.asc
root@bdaa1d27444a:/var/www/html#
root@bdaa1d27444a:/var/www/html# docker-php-source extract
root@bdaa1d27444a:/var/www/html#
root@bdaa1d27444a:/var/www/html# ls -l /usr/src | grep php
drwxr-xr-x 16 root root     4096 Mar  3 18:03 php
-rw-r--r--  1 root root 10418352 Mar  2 04:55 php.tar.xz
-rw-r--r--  1 root root      833 Mar  2 04:55 php.tar.xz.asc
root@bdaa1d27444a:/var/www/html#
```

上面没有 mysqli 模块，安装mysqli拓展。

配置目录准备好：
> mkdir -p /usr/local/etc/php/conf.d

输入：
> docker-php-ext-install mysqli

```

Libraries have been installed in:
   /usr/src/php/ext/mysqli/modules

If you ever happen to want to link against installed libraries
in a given directory, LIBDIR, you must either use libtool, and
specify the full pathname of the library, or use the `-LLIBDIR'
flag during linking and do at least one of the following:
   - add LIBDIR to the `LD_LIBRARY_PATH' environment variable
     during execution
   - add LIBDIR to the `LD_RUN_PATH' environment variable
     during linking
   - use the `-Wl,--rpath -Wl,LIBDIR' linker flag
   - have your system administrator add LIBDIR to `/etc/ld.so.conf'

See any operating system documentation about shared libraries for
more information, such as the ld(1) and ld.so(8) manual pages.

#### gd拓展安装

更新软件源
> apt update

安装各种库
> apt install -y libwebp-dev libjpeg-dev libpng-dev libfreetype6-dev

解压源码
> docker-php-source extract

gd源码文件夹
> cd /usr/src/php/ext/gd

准备编译
```
docker-php-ext-configure gd --with-webp-dir=/usr/include/webp --with-jpeg-dir=/usr/include --with-png-dir=/usr/include --with-freetype-dir=/usr/include/freetype2
```

编译安装
> docker-php-ext-install gd

```

 cc -I/usr/src/php/ext/gd/libgd -I. -I/usr/src/php/ext/gd -DPHP_ATOM_INC -I/usr/src/php/ext/gd/include -I/usr/src/php/ext/gd/main -I/usr/src/php/ext/gd -I/usr/local/include/php -I/usr/local/include/php/main -I/usr/local/include/php/TSRM -I/usr/local/include/php/Zend -I/usr/local/include/php/ext -I/usr/local/include/php/ext/date/lib -I/usr/include/libpng16 -fstack-protector-strong -fpic -fpie -O2 -D_LARGEFILE_SOURCE -D_FILE_OFFSET_BITS=64 -DHAVE_CONFIG_H -fstack-protector-strong -fpic -fpie -O2 -D_LARGEFILE_SOURCE -D_FILE_OFFSET_BITS=64 -c /usr/src/php/ext/gd/gd.c  -fPIC -DPIC -o .libs/gd.o

#### redis拓展安装

> pecl install redis-4.3.0

里面有两个选择：
```
enable igbinary serializer support? [no] : no
enable lzf compression support? [no] : no
```

> docker-php-ext-enable redis

#### swoole拓展安装

安装过程中，有四个可选依赖拓展：
* sockets
* openssl
* http2
* mysqlnd

如果sockets拓展没有安装，可以安装下：
> docker-php-ext-install sockets

swoole拓展对php版本有要求，swoole-4.6版本以上需要php7.2，我们这里安装swoole-4.5.10：
> pecl install swoole-4.5.10

里面有四个选择：
```
enable sockets supports? [no] : yes
enable openssl support? [no] : yes
enable http2 support? [no] : no
enable mysqlnd support? [no] : yes
```

启用swoole拓展：
> docker-php-ext-enable swoole

If you ever happen to want to link against installed libraries
in a given directory, LIBDIR, you must either use libtool, and
specify the full pathname of the library, or use the `-LLIBDIR'
flag during linking and do at least one of the following:
   - add LIBDIR to the `LD_LIBRARY_PATH' environment variable
     during execution
   - add LIBDIR to the `LD_RUN_PATH' environment variable
     during linking
   - use the `-Wl,--rpath -Wl,LIBDIR' linker flag
   - have your system administrator add LIBDIR to `/etc/ld.so.conf'

See any operating system documentation about shared libraries for

#### 删除容器

退出容器后，停止并删除容器
> docker stop php-fpm-7.4
>
> docker rm php-fpm-7.4

### 全新安装

把容器挂载的目录准备好：
> mkdir /etc/php-fpm7.4

```

创建容器并运行
```
docker run --name php-fpm7.4 -p 9000:9000 -v /etc/php-fpm7.4:/usr/local/etc/php -v /media/sf_www:/var/www/html -v /etc/localtime:/etc/localtime:ro --privileged=true -d php:7.4-fpm
```

#### 权限

查看共享文件夹所属组，新建用户组，把服务用户追增到该用户组下。
> groupadd -g 995 vboxsf
> 
> usermod -aG vboxsf www-data

```

退出容器后，重启容器：
> exit
> 
> docker restart php-fpm7.4

#### composer安装

进入容器后，切换目录
> cd /usr/local/src

下载composer安装包
> php -r "copy('https://getcomposer.org/installer', 'composer-setup.php');"

校验下载的包，可以不执行(与发行版本有关)
> php -r "if (hash_file('SHA384', 'composer-setup.php') === '544e09ee996cdf60ece3804abc52599c22b1f40f4323403c44d44fdfdd586475ca9813a858088ffbc1f233e9b180f061') { echo 'Installer verified'; } else { echo 'Installer corrupt'; unlink('composer-setup.php'); } echo PHP_EOL;"

安装
> php composer-setup.php

移除安装包
> php -r "unlink('composer-setup.php');" 

查看PATH路径
> cat /etc/profile

移动到环境搜索目录下，重命名为composer
> mv composer.phar /usr/local/bin/composer

查看composer版本
> composer -v

查看当前源地址
> composer config -g -l repo.packagist

设置国内包源
> composer config -g repo.packagist composer https://mirrors.aliyun.com/composer/

具体操作如下：
```

# /etc/profile: system-wide .profile file for the Bourne shell (sh(1))
# and Bourne compatible shells (bash(1), ksh(1), ash(1), ...).

if [ "$(id -u)" -eq 0 ]; then
  PATH="/usr/local/sbin:/usr/local/bin:/usr/sbin:/usr/bin:/sbin:/bin"
else
  PATH="/usr/local/bin:/usr/bin:/bin:/usr/local/games:/usr/games"
fi
export PATH

if [ "${PS1-}" ]; then
  if [ "${BASH-}" ] && [ "$BASH" != "/bin/sh" ]; then
    # The file bash.bashrc already sets the default PS1.
    # PS1='\h:\w\$ '
    if [ -f /etc/bash.bashrc ]; then
      . /etc/bash.bashrc
    fi
  else
    if [ "$(id -u)" -eq 0 ]; then
      PS1='# '
    else
      PS1='$ '
    fi
  fi
fi

if [ -d /etc/profile.d ]; then
  for i in /etc/profile.d/*.sh; do
    if [ -r $i ]; then
      . $i
    fi
  done
  unset i
fi

#### vim安装

一般docker包中，文本编辑命令 vi、vim 的都是缺失的：
```
root@02891538d8c9:~# vi /etc/apt/sources.list
bash: vi: command not found
root@02891538d8c9:~#
root@02891538d8c9:~# vim /etc/apt/sources.list
bash: vim: command not found
root@02891538d8c9:~#
```

直接apt安装会报 未找到包，先要更新源使之生效：
> apt update

```
root@02891538d8c9:~# apt install vim
Reading package lists... Done
Building dependency tree... Done
Reading state information... Done
E: Unable to locate package vim
root@02891538d8c9:~#
root@02891538d8c9:~# apt update
Get:1 http://deb.debian.org/debian bullseye InRelease [116 kB]
Get:2 http://security.debian.org/debian-security bullseye-security InRelease [44.1 kB]
Get:3 http://deb.debian.org/debian bullseye-updates InRelease [39.4 kB]
Get:4 http://deb.debian.org/debian bullseye/main amd64 Packages [8183 kB]
Get:5 http://security.debian.org/debian-security bullseye-security/main amd64 Packages [120 kB]
Get:6 http://deb.debian.org/debian bullseye-updates/main amd64 Packages [2596 B]
Fetched 8505 kB in 1min 36s (88.2 kB/s)
Reading package lists... Done
Building dependency tree... Done
Reading state information... Done
1 package can be upgraded. Run 'apt list --upgradable' to see it.
root@02891538d8c9:~#
```

然后安装 vim：
> apt install vim

#### 更换国内源

上面安装vim时可以看到速度很慢，我们需要更换国内源。

查看系统版本：

    输入`uname -a`，可显示电脑以及操作系统的相关信息。 
    输入 `cat /proc/version`，说明正在运行的内核版本。
    输入 `cat /etc/issue`, 显示的是发行版本信息
    `lsb_release -a` (适用于所有的linux，包括Redhat、SuSE、Debian等发行版，但是在debian下要安装lsb)

```
root@02891538d8c9:~# uname -a
Linux 02891538d8c9 3.10.0-1160.53.1.el7.x86_64 #1 SMP Fri Jan 14 13:59:45 UTC 2022 x86_64 GNU/Linux
root@02891538d8c9:~#
root@02891538d8c9:~# cat /proc/version
Linux version 3.10.0-1160.53.1.el7.x86_64 (mockbuild@kbuilder.bsys.centos.org) (gcc version 4.8.5 20150623 (Red Hat 4.8.5-44) (GCC) ) #1 SMP Fri Jan 14 13:59:45 UTC 2022
root@02891538d8c9:~#
root@02891538d8c9:~# cat /etc/issue
Debian GNU/Linux 11 \n \l

root@02891538d8c9:~#
root@02891538d8c9:~# lsb_release -a
bash: lsb_release: command not found
root@02891538d8c9:~#
```

系统是Debian版Linux，更换国内源：
> cp /etc/apt/sources.list /etc/apt/sources.list.bak
> 
> vim /etc/apt/sources.list

清空内容后，写入 中科大镜像站：
```
deb https://mirrors.ustc.edu.cn/debian/ buster main contrib non-free
deb https://mirrors.ustc.edu.cn/debian/ buster-updates main contrib non-free
deb https://mirrors.ustc.edu.cn/debian/ buster-backports main contrib non-free
deb https://mirrors.ustc.edu.cn/debian-security/ buster/updates main contrib non-free

deb-src https://mirrors.ustc.edu.cn/debian/ buster main contrib non-free
deb-src https://mirrors.ustc.edu.cn/debian/ buster-updates main contrib non-free
deb-src https://mirrors.ustc.edu.cn/debian/ buster-backports main contrib non-free
deb-src https://mirrors.ustc.edu.cn/debian-security/ buster/updates main contrib non-free
```

更新源使之生效：
> apt update

```
root@02891538d8c9:~# apt update

Get:2 https://mirrors.ustc.edu.cn/debian buster-updates InRelease [51.9 kB]

#### zip安装

有些composer包`composer install`安装时，会报错：
```
    Failed to download symfony/polyfill-mbstring from dist: The zip extension and unzip/7z commands are both missing, skipping.
A php.ini file does not exist. You will have to create one.
    Now trying to download from source
```

zip 和 unzip/7z 命令缺失，我们需要安装这几个软件。

> apt install zip
> 
> apt install unzip
> 
> apt install p7zip

```

#### 拓展安装准备

“源码包”需要放在 /usr/src/php/ext 目录下；默认情况下无 /usr/src/php 这个目录，需要先运行`docker-php-source extract`生成；
docker-php-ext-install安装的扩展，会在 /usr/local/etc/php/conf.d 下写入配置，会自动调用 docker-php-ext-enable 来启用扩展；
卸载扩展，直接删除 /usr/local/etc/php/conf.d 对应的配置文件即可。

初始化php源码目录：
> docker-php-source extract

配置目录准备好：
> mkdir -p /usr/local/etc/php/conf.d

```
root@02891538d8c9:~# php -m
[PHP Modules]

ctype
curl
date
dom

[Zend Modules]

root@02891538d8c9:~#
root@02891538d8c9:~# ls -l /usr/src | grep php
-rw-r--r-- 1 root root 10418352 Mar  2 04:55 php.tar.xz
-rw-r--r-- 1 root root      833 Mar  2 04:55 php.tar.xz.asc
root@02891538d8c9:~#
root@02891538d8c9:~# docker-php-source extract
root@02891538d8c9:~#

root@02891538d8c9:~#
root@02891538d8c9:~# mkdir -p /usr/local/etc/php/conf.d
root@02891538d8c9:~#
root@02891538d8c9:~#
```

#### gd拓展安装

安装各种库
> apt install -y libwebp-dev libjpeg-dev libpng-dev libfreetype6-dev

准备编译（7.4版本的php除了webp、jpg格式和freetype，其他的格式已经不需要单独设置了）
```
> docker-php-ext-configure gd --with-webp=/usr/include/webp --with-jpeg=/usr/include --with-freetype=/usr/include/freetype2
```

编译安装
> docker-php-ext-install gd

```

specify the full pathname of the library, or use the `-LLIBDIR'
flag during linking and do at least one of the following:
   - add LIBDIR to the `LD_LIBRARY_PATH' environment variable
     during execution
   - add LIBDIR to the `LD_RUN_PATH' environment variable
     during linking
   - use the `-Wl,--rpath -Wl,LIBDIR' linker flag
   - have your system administrator add LIBDIR to `/etc/ld.so.conf'

/bin/bash /usr/src/php/ext/pdo_mysql/libtool --mode=link cc -DPHP_ATOM_INC -I/usr/src/php/ext/pdo_mysql/include -I/usr/src/php/ext/pdo_mysql/main -I/usr/src/php/ext/pdo_mysql -I/usr/local/include/php -I/usr/local/include/php/main -I/usr/local/include/php/TSRM -I/usr/local/include/php/Zend -I/usr/local/include/php/ext -I/usr/local/include/php/ext/date/lib  -fstack-protector-strong -fpic -fpie -O2 -D_LARGEFILE_SOURCE -D_FILE_OFFSET_BITS=64 -DHAVE_CONFIG_H  -fstack-protector-strong -fpic -fpie -O2 -D_LARGEFILE_SOURCE -D_FILE_OFFSET_BITS=64  -Wl,-O1 -pie  -o pdo_mysql.la -export-dynamic -avoid-version -prefer-pic -module -rpath /usr/src/php/ext/pdo_mysql/modules  pdo_mysql.lo mysql_driver.lo mysql_statement.lo
cc -shared  .libs/pdo_mysql.o .libs/mysql_driver.o .libs/mysql_statement.o   -Wl,-O1 -Wl,-soname -Wl,pdo_mysql.so -o .libs/pdo_mysql.so

## Nginx容器

在上面 Nginx容器 运行时，我们连接的是 server-php容器：
```
docker run --name server-nginx -p 80:80 -v /media/sf_www:/usr/share/nginx/html -v /etc/localtime:/etc/localtime:ro --link server-php:php --privileged=true -d nginx
```

这里我们要重新运行一个 Nginx容器，连接 php-fpm7.4容器：
```
docker run --name nginx-php7.4 -p 80:80 -v /media/sf_www:/usr/share/nginx/html -v /etc/localtime:/etc/localtime:ro --link php-fpm7.4:php --privileged=true -d nginx
```

```
[root@localhost ~]# docker run --name nginx-php7.4 -p 80:80 -v /media/sf_www:/usr/share/nginx/html -v /etc/localtime:/etc/localtime:ro --link php-fpm7.4:php --privileged=true -d nginx
9990da899f8e236aa6c2b11ac86e1830a35db543d35e424da481809ed1e59e21
[root@localhost ~]#
[root@localhost ~]# docker ps -a

### vim安装

进入server-nginx容器：
> docker exec -it nginx-php7.4 /bin/bash

更新源使之生效：
> apt update

```

### conf配置

编辑 /etc/nginx/nginx.conf：
> vim /etc/nginx/nginx.conf

把 `include /etc/nginx/conf.d/*.conf;` 修改为 `include /usr/share/nginx/html/vhost/virtualbox/docker/*.conf;` 。
